<th scope="row">Area</th>
<td>30,370,000 km<sup>2</sup> (11,730,000 sq mi), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_continents_by_area" title="List of continents by area">2nd</a></td>

<tr>
<th scope="row">Population</th>
<td>1,225,080,510<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UN_WPP_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-UN_WPP-1">[1]</a></sup> (2016, <a href="/wiki/List_of_continents_by_population" title="List of continents by population">2nd</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Population density</th>
<td>36.4/km<sup>2</sup> (94/sq mi)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">GDP (nominal)</th>
<td>US$3.3 trillion (2017, <a href="/wiki/List_of_continents_by_GDP_(nominal)" title="List of continents by GDP (nominal)">5th</a>)</td>
</tr>

<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria"><img alt="Nigeria" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="800" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/35px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/46px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Ibadan" title="Ibadan">Ibadan</a><br/>
<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya"><img alt="Kenya" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Kenya.svg/23px-Flag_of_Kenya.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Kenya.svg/35px-Flag_of_Kenya.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Kenya.svg/45px-Flag_of_Kenya.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Nairobi" title="Nairobi">Nairobi</a><br/>
<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria"><img alt="Nigeria" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="800" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/35px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/46px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Abuja" title="Abuja">Abuja</a><br/>
<span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Ghana" title="Ghana"><img alt="Ghana" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Ghana.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ghana.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Ghana.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ghana.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Flag_of_Ghana.svg/45px-Flag_of_Ghana.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Accra" title="Accra">Accra</a></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>Africa</b> is the world's second-largest and second-most-populous <a href="/wiki/Continent" title="Continent">continent</a> (the first being <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a>). At about 30.3 million km<sup>2</sup> (11.7 million square miles) including adjacent islands, it covers 6% of <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth's</a> total surface area and 20.4% of its total land area.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sayre_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sayre-2">[2]</a></sup> With 1.2 billion<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UN_WPP_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-UN_WPP-1">[1]</a></sup> people as of 2016, it accounts for about 16% of the world's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Human_population" title="Human population">human population</a>. The continent is surrounded by the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">Mediterranean Sea</a> to the north, both the <a href="/wiki/Suez_Canal" title="Suez Canal">Suez Canal</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Red_Sea" title="Red Sea">Red Sea</a> along the <a href="/wiki/Sinai_Peninsula" title="Sinai Peninsula">Sinai Peninsula</a> to the northeast, the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a> to the southeast and the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic Ocean</a> to the west. The continent includes <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a> and various <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">archipelagos</a>. It contains 54 <a href="/wiki/Diplomatic_recognition" title="Diplomatic recognition">fully recognised</a> <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign states</a> (<a href="/wiki/Country" title="Country">countries</a>), nine <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Territory_(country_subdivision)" title="Territory (country subdivision)">territories</a> and two <i><a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a></i> independent <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">states with limited or no recognition</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>Africa's average population is the youngest amongst all the continents;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Median" title="Median">median</a> age in 2012 was 19.7, when the worldwide median age was 30.4.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> is Africa's largest country by area, and <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> is its largest by population. Africa, particularly central <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Africa" title="Eastern Africa">Eastern Africa</a>, is widely accepted as the place of origin of <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">humans</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Hominidae" title="Hominidae">Hominidae</a> <a href="/wiki/Clade" title="Clade">clade</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Great_ape" title="Great ape">great apes</a>), as <a href="/wiki/Evidence" title="Evidence">evidenced</a> by the discovery of the earliest <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hominids" title="Hominids">hominids</a> and their ancestors, as well as later ones that have been dated to around seven million years ago, including <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sahelanthropus_tchadensis" title="Sahelanthropus tchadensis">Sahelanthropus tchadensis</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Australopithecus_africanus" title="Australopithecus africanus">Australopithecus africanus</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Australopithecus_afarensis" title="Australopithecus afarensis">A. afarensis</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_erectus" title="Homo erectus">Homo erectus</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_habilis" title="Homo habilis">H. habilis</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_ergaster" title="Homo ergaster">H. ergaster</a></i>—with the earliest <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_sapiens" title="Homo sapiens">Homo sapiens</a></i> (modern human) found in <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> being dated to circa 200,000 years ago.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> Africa straddles the <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">equator</a> and encompasses numerous climate areas; it is the only continent to stretch from the northern <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Temperate" title="Temperate">temperate</a> to southern temperate zones.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></p>
<p>Africa hosts a large diversity of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ethnic_groups_of_Africa" title="Ethnic groups of Africa">ethnicities</a>, cultures and <a href="/wiki/Languages_of_Africa" title="Languages of Africa">languages</a>. In the <a href="/wiki/New_Imperialism" title="New Imperialism">late 19th century</a> European countries <a href="/wiki/Scramble_for_Africa" title="Scramble for Africa">colonised almost all of Africa</a>. Africa also varies greatly with regard to environments, economics, historical ties and government systems. However, most present states in Africa originate from a process of <a href="/wiki/Decolonisation_of_Africa" title="Decolonisation of Africa">decolonisation</a> in the 20th century. African nations have attempted to cooperate through the establishment of the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a>, which is headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Addis_Ababa" title="Addis Ababa">Addis Ababa</a>.</p>
<p></p>
